text: "Sounds of the Singing School. (Round in Five Parts.)\nP. P. BLISS.\n42\nDivide the class into five divisions and number them, (make two divisions of Soprano or any part that is most numerous) First division sings first staff alone. When\nfirst division begins second staff, second division begins piece. When second division begins second staff, and first division third staff, third division begins piece, and\nso on. Sing the piece through twice, the divisions ending one after another as they begin, or together at the end of any staff all singing the word \"away.\" The teacher\nmay make a vocal training exercise of this by calling out while they are singing,-\"piano, forte, cres., dim., legato, staccato, forzando, clear, somber,\" &c.\n\352\270\260\nN\nNow for a song of the singing school, And the sounds you there may hear,\nla la la la la la la la la la la\nKeep\nre\nthe\n240\nmi\nAccompaniment.\nfa\ntime with\nOh, ah, a, e, bo,bah, ba,be,\nsol la si do\n\342\202\254\ngg\nla la la la la la la la la la la\n80\ncont\n1s the ma\nSit up erect,\nstrong,\nI\nOf the do re mi and the G A B and the voi-ces ringing clear.\nH\njor scale, you know,\nsay,\nLines and spaces, clefs and keys,\nFull and clear\nHo,ho, ho,\n!!!\n12\nthe\nha, ha, ha,\nE\nAll must tell with ease.\nEv-en,double,triple measure too,are among the many unings we do.\ntones\nUNA\nH\npro -long.\n111\nDrive dull care a- way.\nEl"
